    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-u_xlat0.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = clamp(u_xlat15, 0.0, 1.0);

vec4 u_xlat0;

mediump float u_xlat16_35;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _EnvOffset.xyz * vec3(0.0174532924, 0.0174532924, 0.0174532924);
    u_xlat3.xyz = cos(u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = sin(u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zyx * u_xlat3.xxz;
    u_xlat5.xy = u_xlat2.yz * u_xlat2.xx;
    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat3.z + u_xlat4.x;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat3.zzy * u_xlat3.yxx;
    u_xlat6.y = (-u_xlat5.x) * u_xlat2.z + u_xlat7.y;
    u_xlat5.x = (-u_xlat4.y) * u_xlat3.z + u_xlat5.y;
    u_xlat5.y = u_xlat4.y * u_xlat2.z + u_xlat4.z;
    u_xlat6.z = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat3.y;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = u_xlat7.z;
    u_xlat4.z = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat7.y = u_xlat2.z * (-u_xlat3.y);
    u_xlat7.z = u_xlat2.y;
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_35 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_35);

    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat2.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;

    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xzw = u_xlat16_8.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_17)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_8.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_8.z;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;

    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_2.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_6.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_6.xy;

    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;

    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;

    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + u_xlat0.x;

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat15 = min(max(u_xlat15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat15 = clamp(u_xlat15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_3.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * 6.0;

    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = exp2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ReflacMul.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(_ReflecPow);

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _LightColor.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_1.w;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;

    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);

    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-u_xlat0.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = clamp(u_xlat15, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_3.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_1 = textureCube(_EnvCubeMap, u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat10_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = exp2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_BaseColor, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ReflacMul.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(_ReflecPow);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-_FresnelColor.xyz) + _FresnelColor2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat16_4.xyz + _FresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * _LightColor.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_1.w;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_3.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;

vec4 u_xlat0;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;

vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
vec3 u_xlat6;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_8;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat27;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _EnvOffset.xyz * vec3(0.0174532924, 0.0174532924, 0.0174532924);
    u_xlat3.xyz = cos(u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = sin(u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zyx * u_xlat3.xxz;
    u_xlat5.xy = u_xlat2.yz * u_xlat2.xx;
    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat3.z + u_xlat4.x;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat3.zzy * u_xlat3.yxx;
    u_xlat6.y = (-u_xlat5.x) * u_xlat2.z + u_xlat7.y;
    u_xlat5.x = (-u_xlat4.y) * u_xlat3.z + u_xlat5.y;
    u_xlat5.y = u_xlat4.y * u_xlat2.z + u_xlat4.z;
    u_xlat6.z = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat3.y;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = u_xlat7.z;
    u_xlat4.z = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat7.y = u_xlat2.z * (-u_xlat3.y);
    u_xlat7.z = u_xlat2.y;
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_35 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_35) + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_1.y;
    u_xlat16_8.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_8.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_8.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_1;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat2.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_8.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xzw = u_xlat16_8.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_17)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_8.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_8.z;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat2.xxxx;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0 = min(max(u_xlat0, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0 = clamp(u_xlat0, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = u_xlat0;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_2.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-u_xlat0.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_3.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(_EnvCubeMap, u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = exp2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BaseColor, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ReflacMul.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(_ReflecPow);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _FresnelColor2.xyz + (-_FresnelColor2a.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = _IFFLIP * -2.0 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_21 = _PostUVFlip1 * u_xlat16_21 + _IFFLIP;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_4.xyz + _FresnelColor2a.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = _FresnelColor.xyz + (-_FresnelColora.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + _FresnelColora.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + (-u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _LightColor.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_1.w;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_3.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    return;

varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;

vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_8;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat27;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _EnvOffset.xyz * vec3(0.0174532924, 0.0174532924, 0.0174532924);
    u_xlat3.xyz = cos(u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = sin(u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zyx * u_xlat3.xxz;
    u_xlat5.xy = u_xlat2.yz * u_xlat2.xx;
    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat3.z + u_xlat4.x;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat3.zzy * u_xlat3.yxx;
    u_xlat6.y = (-u_xlat5.x) * u_xlat2.z + u_xlat7.y;
    u_xlat5.x = (-u_xlat4.y) * u_xlat3.z + u_xlat5.y;
    u_xlat5.y = u_xlat4.y * u_xlat2.z + u_xlat4.z;
    u_xlat6.z = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat3.y;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = u_xlat7.z;
    u_xlat4.z = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat7.y = u_xlat2.z * (-u_xlat3.y);
    u_xlat7.z = u_xlat2.y;
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_35 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_35) + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;

    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat2.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;

    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_17)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_8.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_8.z;

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;

    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];

    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;

    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_3.x;

    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * _LightColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_1.w;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_24) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;

    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);

    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);

#endif

    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * 6.0;

    u_xlat16_3.x = exp2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ReflacMul.xyz;

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _FresnelColor2.xyz + (-_FresnelColor2a.xyz);
    u_xlat16_24 = _IFFLIP * -2.0 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_24 = _PostUVFlip1 * u_xlat16_24 + _IFFLIP;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_24) * u_xlat16_4.xyz + _FresnelColor2a.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = _FresnelColor.xyz + (-_FresnelColora.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_24) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + _FresnelColora.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + (-u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_24 = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * _LightColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_1.w;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_24) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    return;

    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-u_xlat0.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_3.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_1 = textureCube(_EnvCubeMap, u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat10_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = exp2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_BaseColor, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ReflacMul.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(_ReflecPow);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-_FresnelColor.xyz) + _FresnelColor2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat16_4.xyz + _FresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat16_24 = u_xlat10_0.w;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * _LightColor.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_1.w;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_24) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_3.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    return;
}

#endif
"

    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);

    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz / u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + (-unity_FogColor.xyz);
    SV_Target0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD11.www * u_xlat16_3.xyz + unity_FogColor.xyz;
    return;
}

#endif

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D unity_Lightmap;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _BaseColor;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump samplerCube _EnvCubeMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
float u_xlat21;
mediump float u_xlat16_24;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_2.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_8.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_8.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-u_xlat0.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat21 = min(max(u_xlat21, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_3.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(_EnvCubeMap, u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_3.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = log2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_3.x = exp2(u_xlat16_3.x);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BaseColor, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ReflacMul.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(_ReflecPow);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _FresnelColor2.xyz + (-_FresnelColor2a.xyz);
    u_xlat16_24 = _IFFLIP * -2.0 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_24 = _PostUVFlip1 * u_xlat16_24 + _IFFLIP;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_24) * u_xlat16_4.xyz + _FresnelColor2a.xyz;

	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_ProbesOcclusion;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _UVScallePaner;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RenderType;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cull;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZWrite;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _ZTest;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AlphaToMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SrcBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactorAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BlendOpAlpha;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _FresnelColora;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _LightColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EnvOffset;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_8;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat27;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = _EnvOffset.xyz * vec3(0.0174532924, 0.0174532924, 0.0174532924);
    u_xlat3.xyz = cos(u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = sin(u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zyx * u_xlat3.xxz;
    u_xlat5.xy = u_xlat2.yz * u_xlat2.xx;
    u_xlat6.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat3.z + u_xlat4.x;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat3.zzy * u_xlat3.yxx;
    u_xlat6.y = (-u_xlat5.x) * u_xlat2.z + u_xlat7.y;
    u_xlat5.x = (-u_xlat4.y) * u_xlat3.z + u_xlat5.y;
    u_xlat5.y = u_xlat4.y * u_xlat2.z + u_xlat4.z;
    u_xlat6.z = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat3.y;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat6.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = u_xlat7.z;
    u_xlat4.z = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat7.y = u_xlat2.z * (-u_xlat3.y);
    u_xlat7.z = u_xlat2.y;
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_35 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_35) + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_1.y;
    u_xlat16_8.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_8.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_8.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_1;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat2.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_8.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_17 = u_xlat16_8.x * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xzw = u_xlat16_8.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_17)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_8.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_8.z;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainLightShadowParams;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DstBlendFactorAlpha;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _FresnelColora;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _LightColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EnvOffset;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BaseColor;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump samplerCube _EnvCubeMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
bool u_xlatb6;
mediump float u_xlat16_7;
mediump float u_xlat16_13;
float u_xlat23;
void main()
{
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(vs_TEXCOORD7.xy,vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
    u_xlat16_0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb6 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb6 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb6 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_7 = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7 = min(max(u_xlat16_7, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7 = clamp(u_xlat16_7, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_2.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_3.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_7) * u_xlat16_3.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_7);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_7) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat16_0.y * u_xlat16_0.y;
    u_xlat16_7 = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x + (-u_xlat16_7);
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_0.yzzx * u_xlat16_0.xyzz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = dot(unity_SHBr, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.y = dot(unity_SHBg, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.z = dot(unity_SHBb, u_xlat16_2);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = unity_SHC.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_7) + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(unity_SHAr, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(unity_SHAg, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(unity_SHAb, u_xlat16_0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_BaseColor, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _LightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = (-u_xlat16_13) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_13 * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_13 * 6.0;
    u_xlat5.x = dot((-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x + u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * (-u_xlat5.xxx) + (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
    u_xlat23 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat23 = min(max(u_xlat23, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat23 = clamp(u_xlat23, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = textureLod(_EnvCubeMap, u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_13);
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_0.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_13 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_13 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_13 = max(u_xlat16_13, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_13 = log2(u_xlat16_13);
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_13 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_13 = exp2(u_xlat16_13);
    u_xlat16_13 = u_xlat16_13 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_13);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_2.w;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _ReflacMul.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(_ReflecPow);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-_FresnelColor.xyz) + _FresnelColor2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat23) * u_xlat16_4.xyz + _FresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat5.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat5.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;

vec3 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_8;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat27;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;

    u_xlat1.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat1.xyz;

    u_xlat2.xyz = sin(u_xlat2.xyz);

    u_xlat5.xy = u_xlat2.yz * u_xlat2.xx;

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_35 = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat16_8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_35);

    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);

    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_8.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_8.z;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat27 = max(u_xlat27, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat27 = inversesqrt(u_xlat27);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);

#endif

#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];

attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;

float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);

    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
